<div id="review_1423288245" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1423288245" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1423288245?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Pearl by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga">Beatrice Masaluñga</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=sobfest">sobfest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=mind-blown">mind-blown</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=annoying-heroines">annoying-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=highly-recommended-na">highly-recommended-na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=hot-male-characters">hot-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=smexy-read">smexy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1423288245" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3915890352756940968"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I've fallen in love with another man. But can you love two men at the same time? Because I think I do.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>I AM A COMPLETE MESS RIGHT NOW.</b> My emotions have never been so conflicted. What did this book do to me?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446862170ra/16914348.gif' width='250' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is the kind of book that I should not have loved, yet I ended up thoroughly appreciating it just because... <b>the ending!</b><br/><br/>I have to give the author <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7112180.Mia_Asher' title='Mia Asher' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mia Asher</a> a lot of credit for giving me all kinds of emotions all throughout the book. This book is clearly <b>WRONG</b> when it comes to it</span>
  <span id="freeText3915890352756940968" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I've fallen in love with another man. But can you love two men at the same time? Because I think I do.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>I AM A COMPLETE MESS RIGHT NOW.</b> My emotions have never been so conflicted. What did this book do to me?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446862170ra/16914348.gif" width="250" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is the kind of book that I should not have loved, yet I ended up thoroughly appreciating it just because... <b>the ending!</b><br><br>I have to give the author <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7112180.Mia_Asher" title="Mia Asher" rel="nofollow noopener">Mia Asher</a> a lot of credit for giving me all kinds of emotions all throughout the book. This book is clearly <b>WRONG</b> when it comes to its concept which is <b>CHEATING</b> but quite honestly, after reading it, I've realized that behind the lies, the deception, and the betrayal <b>Cathy</b> did to her husband, the book gave a very powerful and overriding message to everyone. That indeed, doing these things will not only destroy your relationship with your partner, but it will also destroy you as a person.<br><br>The story is all about the perfect married couple <b>Cathy</b> and <b>Ben</b>. They have the marriage everyone is dreaming of. Ben loves Cathy completely and wholeheartedly. And even when Cathy had so many miscarriages all throughout their marriage, he was still the same devoted husband. However, Cathy slowly became depressed when the third baby became a failure. Then Cathy met the gorgeous and attractive blonde <b>Arsen</b> who made her heart and body confused. When her next miscarriage happened, that's when her entire world crumbled and she did the worst mistake of her life...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I'm done with doing the right thing. It's at this moment, when I feel Arsen’s hot breath on my face and his arms wrapped around me, that I decide to throw everything away. Ben, my marriage, my future.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br>Cathy cheated and completely forgot her perfect husband and everything about their marriage just to be with Arsen who gave her all the pleasure a man could offer. Honestly, <b>I HATED CATHY</b>. And I still do. What she did was choose <i>lust</i> over love. I wanted to strangle her just to bring her back to her senses because she was such an ingrate, very selfish woman. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Arsen was the fuel needed to burn my marriage to the ground, but I was the one who held the match in my hands the entire time.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>But what made this book sensational was the soul-wrenching emotions it gave me as a reader. I felt every word and every line deep down in my core. Mia Asher is an emotional genius! <b>Her words are like daggers</b> that when you read them, they will not just make you wince in pain but destroy your heart for what it's worth. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446864791ra/16915580.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441924055ra/16168374.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The best part of this book was the ending. It was, in a way, a different kind of twist. It was not a very pleasant conclusion. It was bitter-sweet but it was worth it and I think that's the best way to end this super sad, heart-breaking book. Kudos to Mia Asher for turning me into an emotional mess!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Arsen became the air I needed to breathe, but Ben was my lungs.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Rating:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445994440i/16731146.jpg" width="200" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p>
  <a href="https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446199662i/16763926._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pearl's Book Journey (1)" width="380" height="190" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445993261i/16730770.jpg" width="200" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="3915890352756940968" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11162852-alessandra-torre?shelf=suggested-for-readers">suggested-for-readers</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer714765477" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4534025683767830341">This book took me through a rollercoaster of emotions. I didn't enjoy it the entire time, but I <i>felt</i> the entire time, and for that reason, I give it 5 stars. I would def recommend it - especially for readers that like cheating, love triangles, and angst.<br/><br/>Note: I didn't develop an attachment for Arsen, and never really cared for the female lead, but despite those major stumbling blocks, I still really enjoyed the book.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <blockquote>No </blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText855715219163303626" style="display:none"><br><br><br><b> LOVE HAS THE POWER TO DESTROY YOU. </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432945i/870915._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reviewing this book isn’t easy. Ben &amp; Cathy fell in love more than ten years ago. Their first encounter put a silly grin on my face every time I think about it. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>He is the everything to my nothing</blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432945ra/870916.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After all those years together their relationship is not the same.<br> <br><b>
  <blockquote>No one has all the answers to solve the big puzzle that life is, and it is even less likely that another person can offer them to you.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Cathy and Ben are trying to have a baby but they have had three miscarriages. For this reason their marriage is not the same after all those years. Cathy blames her own body for not being able to hold a baby during 9 months and Ben is that kind of guy who’s always positive and calm, who is always telling you everything will be ok. Sometimes that kind of men might become annoying because even though they are trying their best to keep you happy, listening to their “crap” isn’t helping.<br><br>And then Arsen enters the picture. Arsen is a spoiled young man who has the world at his feet. He can have every woman he wants but he wants Cathy and Cathy is not available because she loves her husband, right?<br> <br><b>
  <blockquote>”Live without love, without chasing your dreams, is nothing. It means nothing. It’s a sad fucking empty shell, Catherine. It’s so easy to drown in darkness, to let it smother you, swallow you whole, to be blinded by it. But you gotta fight. You gotta fucking fight.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>This is all you are going to get from me about their story. The below are just my crazy thoughts and I am going to <b>BEG you to do NOT open the spoilers</b> because I’ll ruin the book for you and I want you all to give this story a try and go blind.<br><br>There are books that hit close to home. Not only because whatever happens in the story happened to you already but because you learn things from some stories. If you know how to learn between lines I guess you’ll end up <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ appreciating what you have in your life. I am now posting this review with my “Ben” sitting beside me and while I’ve had doubts before during our 9 years relationship, I am glad I ended up valuing what we have.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I can’t say my life is any similar to Cathy’s, no Arsens on my life but I understand her somehow. Yeah, I said I understand Cathy and Cathy is a cheater. <b>Now, if you stop judging</b> I would like to explain myself.<br><br>I mentioned before that things were not the same for Cathy &amp; Ben after more than 10 years together and this didn’t surprise me. <b>WHAT? You ladies think being in a long term relationship with someone is like some authors describe it in books? Oh well… let me break your bubble.</b> When you are on a long term relationship you have good days but you also have bad days and sometimes you question your feelings, sometimes you need something (I didn’t say someone) new, sometimes you just get bored. It doesn’t mean you don’t love that person, it means you are H-U-M-A-N. End of.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Every action has a consequence. It doesn’t matter if you try to run or hide. It eventually catches up to you. Call it karma if you must, but said karma can totally kick you in the ass</blockquote>
</b><br><br>The right thing to do in that situation you ask? I guess the right thing to do is just having a conversation with your boyfriend/hubby and explaining them what’s going on with your feelings. But that’s not easy and we all make mistakes, especially when temptation is knocking on your door. I didn’t like Cathy because she hurt Ben and sometimes it looked like she didn’t even care for him after all those years but somehow I understood her. She felt ALIVE again when she met Arsen and he taught her another side of life, a side she had long ago forgotten.<br> <br><b>
  <blockquote>”Falling in love with someone is easy. It’s loving when the newness has worn off, when life gets tough, when things get in the way, when physical passion is gone, that true love remains. When love can conquer it all”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>There is a song that was playing in my mind all the time while reading this book. Pls check this link and this song by The Killers. FOR REASONS UNKNOWN. Especially I beg you to check minute 3:16 and listen to what Brandon says. Because that song feels very real. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I have been there and it’s ok, it doesn’t mean you can’t save your relationship, you still can if you want.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> But the sad truth is, relationships are not like in books and that’s why I loved this book because this is not a heart and flowers story, this is a BROKEN love story.<br><br><b><a>FOR REASONS UNKNOWN BY THE KILLERS</a> </b><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<br>“Any of you people ever loved somebody?<br>Sometimes it comes very quickly, very easily<br>and sometimes it disappears just as quick.<br>You wake up one morning,<br>the butterflies stop fluttering,<br>but you want it back and you want to fight for it.<br>You wanna breathe that fire again<br>so you call for it, you call out.”<br> </blockquote>
</b><br><br>There is just ONE REASON why this book didn’t get a higher rating from me. I wish ***PLEASE I BEG YOU TO DO NOT OPEN THE SPOILER IF YOU HAVEN’T READ THIS BOOK. I’LL RUIN THE END FOR YOU *** <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Cathy would have realized she still loved Ben while being with Arsen. It felt like she started realizing about her feelings for Ben just because Arsen left her and ended their “relationship”. Anyway I loved their story…  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Thanks Helena for our BR &amp; THANKS ANA RITA for laughing at my crazy theories...<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="855715219163303626" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_638777400" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/638777400" />
    <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/638777400?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=the-hype-is-a-lie">the-hype-is-a-lie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=scorching-hot">scorching-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=i-m-a-quitter">i-m-a-quitter</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer638777400" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11627101867150045444">To be fair I am rating this book as I do all of my DNF books. <br/><br/>DNF at 46%. Let it be known that I DNF'd this book <b>PRIOR</b> to any cheating taking place. I knew going in to the book that it had cheating--which I hate--and decided to give it a shot based on all of the high ratings. However, the cheating was not my biggest issue.<br/><br/>Unfortunately the heroine Cathy was my biggest issue. She was one of the worst book heroines to date. I didn't like the Cathy in the past or present chapters. She was annoying,</span>
  <span id="freeText11627101867150045444" style="display:none">To be fair I am rating this book as I do all of my DNF books. <br /><br />DNF at 46%. Let it be known that I DNF'd this book <b>PRIOR</b> to any cheating taking place. I knew going in to the book that it had cheating--which I hate--and decided to give it a shot based on all of the high ratings. However, the cheating was not my biggest issue.<br /><br />Unfortunately the heroine Cathy was my biggest issue. She was one of the worst book heroines to date. I didn't like the Cathy in the past or present chapters. She was annoying, immature and just made one dumb decision after another. She was very contradictory throughout the book with regards to her feelings for Ben....one minute internalizing how bored and unhappy she is with Ben and her marriage yet in the next breath talking about how much she misses her husband and can't wait to get home to him. <br /><br />IDK, I just didn't feel the disconnect that warranted her cheating or thinking of cheating or whatever. I understand, or can imagine, how hard it must be to go through multiple miscarriages....however, I wish she just would have talked to Ben about how she was feeling. He lost those babies too and he was so supportive of Cathy. I seriously loved Ben and knew that he was the one that was going to suffer the most from everything. Angst and drama caused by lack of communication is one of my biggest peeves!!!!<br /><br />Now for Arsen....I honestly did not like him either. From the beginning he was an arrogant womanizing ass. I didn't feel any connection between him and Cathy....not even the friendship. And the one interaction he had with Ben was just awful. I can't imagine why Cathy would want to cheat on Ben with him. For me, he didn't bring anything positive to the table. <br /><br />I could envision how the story was going to go. I did skim to the end to see who she ended up with. If it were up to me, Cathy would end up alone. The bits I was able to piece together makes me glad that I didn't finish. I shouldn't have even read it to begin with but I'm glad that I stopped when I did. Ben gets 5 stars.....Cathy, Arsen and the story itself gets 1. I will say, the writing was strong and I would consider other works by this author as a result.....just perhaps with a different storyline and hopefully a more redeeming heroine. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11627101867150045444" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_703115493" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/703115493" />
    <a title="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7530032-jessica-angie-jessica-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508375424p2/7530032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/703115493?book_show_action=true">Aug 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" href="/user/show/7530032-jessica-angie-jessica-s-dreamy-reads">Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer703115493" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13165365678561525427">If I'm being completely honest, I didn't love this book. I'm not even sure I liked it. But to explain myself, I have to include major spoilers, so read on at your own discretion... <br/><br/>Before everyone starts throwing things, let me be clear. I love love love a good love triangle. I love a bad boy. I love cursing and bad language and dirty sex. I love an angst-ridden emotional roller coaster. I love darkness and pain. I love my heart to break. So before you think I read a book outside of my genre of </span>
  <span id="freeText13165365678561525427" style="display:none">If I'm being completely honest, I didn't love this book. I'm not even sure I liked it. But to explain myself, I have to include major spoilers, so read on at your own discretion... <br /><br />Before everyone starts throwing things, let me be clear. I love love love a good love triangle. I love a bad boy. I love cursing and bad language and dirty sex. I love an angst-ridden emotional roller coaster. I love darkness and pain. I love my heart to break. So before you think I read a book outside of my genre of choice and then berated the crap out of it, let me be clear: this was SO right up my ally. It just... wasn't it for me... <br /><br />First off, I hated Cathy. And when you hate your main character, when you hate the sound of her voice and her inner monologue, I'm not sure where you can go from there. From the age of 18, at that party, where Ben was nothing but a stand-up respectful, honorable guy and wanted to wait to have sex with Cathy in a romantic, respectable way, and Cathy pitched a tantrum, dressed like a whore, danced like a skank with Ben's friend who she'd never met, just to try to make Ben jealous... Honestly... I can not be Team Cathy after that juvenile display of deplorable behavior. 22 year old, law school bound Ben should have dropped Cathy's stupid ass right then and there. But he didn't.<br /><br />And maybe that whole episode was supposed to allude to how Cathy would handle stress later in life and act out on it instead of dealing with it head on... and maybe it was supposed to show how Ben would love her through it despite her flaws... but it dropped Cathy down on my respect meter significantly.<br /><br />And speaking of Ben... I loved Ben. Ben was the only ray of light in this whole dark mess. But when Ben finally, after the whole big fight, and after Cathy's tantrum, decided after all that happened to do Cathy doggy style on a dresser in the upstairs bedroom of a rowdy party... well that did not seem like consistent behavior with the Ben I had come to know and love. This is not something Ben would do. Not his first time with Cathy, not just a day before declaring his love for her... he'd save the doggy for later. Just sayin... So with that said, I proceeded to read while subconsciously looking for holes in the story. <br /><br />Arsen. Now, I will repeat. I love a bad boy. I will, without fail, always always always root for the bad boy in any given situation. Arsen is now the exception to my rule. Arsen is an asshole. I get that he's supposed to be younger than Cathy, early to mid-20s. I get that he is a sexy, wealthy playboy. So do you mean to tell me that no where in that privileged upbringing, no one taught him some tact and etiquette? You don't drop the f-bomb in front of complete strangers. You don't talk about who else you screwed and why and when and how in front of a woman that you are friends with but secretly pining after. I don't know if the author felt that the overuse of the f-bomb was necessary to convey Arsen's masculinity, or his womanizing personality... but it was just that: overused. The overuse made me roll my eyes and it all went from being sexy dialogue to cheesy, gouge out my eyeballs with a fork annoying. <br /><br />Maybe it's my fault that I bought into all the hype on goodreads and facebook about how intensely emotional this book was. But it took way too long to develop, in my opinion. Things didn't pick up until after the 40%ish mark. If I was one of those readers (which I am not!) that abandons a book out of boredom, I would have. <br /><br />But alas, things did pick up. The drama increased and my hate for Cathy multiplied exponentially. Now, don't get me wrong, I sympathized with her loss and her pain. But to put any of the blame on Ben for why the marriage was crumbling was just wrong. He did what any husband in that situation would have done, he stayed strong despite his own pain, he tried to remain positive and he tried to convince Cathy to do the same. But Cathy, once again, decides that the sun and moon rise and fall out of her ass, and she does whatever she wants, despite who she hurts. Now, everyone and their mother hated Kiera because of how wishy washy she was between Kellan and Denny. Cathy knocks wishy washy out of the ball park. I understand the whole loving two guys synopsis. But the whole "I love Ben so much" (blink) "I love Arsen so much" (turn page) "I love Ben"... I mean, really. Atleast mull that shit over a bit. It was LITERALLY, as soon as whoever she was with stopped touching her for 2 seconds, she was madly in love with the other guy. Yet she showed no remorse EVER. Atleast Keira felt badly about what she did to Denny.This chick needed more therapy than Crystle can offer up, she needs to be committed. And calling Amy for advice and then arguing with her because she didn't like what she heard... the selfishness of this chick knows no bounds. Get over yourself. I started to almost think that maybe she couldn't have a child because she wasn't selfless enough to care for one. She wanted a baby more than she wanted anything... including a good man. I just can't find it in myself to like her or want good things for her.<br /><br />My favorite part of the book... the part of the book that pulled me in, and the only part of the book that I had any real emotional connection with, was Ben's emotional breakdown upon Cathy's final admittance. That was heartbreaking and I cried... like real, actual tears. He would have, undoubtedly, forgiven Cathy on the spot if she had shown even an ounce of remorse. But of course she did not. <br /><br />And to top off my already pissed off cake, Cathy doesn't even bother to figure out who fathered that kid?? I mean, come ON! Arsen... ok, fine. He said he didn't want to be a father. We know it was a lie, but if Cathy was basing her actions on what she knew, then Arsen wouldn't have been involved with her or the kid anyway, so atleast you have the truth. But to not find out the truth for Ben's sake? That guy wanted a child and a family just as badly as Cathy did. He suffered those losses just like he did. And she didn't tell him?? That's probably more dispicable than the affair. <br /><br />I was happy with the ending. I was glad that she and Ben ended up together, because ultimately that is the ending I hoped for. But then the epilogue came along and ruined that. I was kinda pissed that Arsen is made out to be some kind of hero at the end, suddenly putting everyone else's happiness before his own. Really, Arsen? Where was your sense of selflessness when you told Cathy to get on her knees in your bedroom. Give me a break. And the fact that Nadia is his makes me even more mad. But whatever... it is what it is... <br /><br />Maybe buying into the hype set my expectations too high. Maybe I'm just a critical reader and hard to please. I don't know why I didn't love this book. I do know that my love or hate of a book is based on how I feel while reading it. I don't have to love the outcome of a book to love the story. I actually live for how many painful tugs my heart feels while reading a book. I look for turmoil and pain and heartbreak. And I know how I was supposed to feel while I read Arsen... I was supposed to feel emotionally torn for Cathy, I was supposed to feel how difficult this life-altering decision is for her to make, how hard it is to choose one love or another. But that's not what I felt. I felt anger toward her for being so selfish and putting herself in this situation to begin with. I felt utter disdain for this chick who would go screw her boyfriend in a closet at a party while her husband practically begged her not to. I could not sympathize with the main character, and I think that obviously affected how I read the entire story. <br /><br />Arsen is the fire and Ben is the rain... and Cathy should be shackled in a basement somewhere and not allowed to experience the weather.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13165365678561525427" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_704087892" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/704087892" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/704087892?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer704087892" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11638768500384184038">Thank God that's over! I finished it!<br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/34p0sj9jpg_zps87d186ba.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434396ra/876201.gif' alt=' photo 34p0sj9jpg_zps87d186ba.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>***Review edited after long deliberation and my inability to get this story out of my head. Any book that knocks my world off its axis deserves a five-star rating versus my initial no-rating. Nothing has changed but my revelation that this author deserves my five stars......</b><br/><br/>Now for my review.....<br/><br/>Sweet Jesus, gimme some Prozac, wine, anything to calm my nerves! I struggled so much with this book. Why? Because I hated "their" story yet I still think it's an</span>
  <span id="freeText11638768500384184038" style="display:none">Thank God that's over! I finished it!<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/34p0sj9jpg_zps87d186ba.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434396ra/876201.gif" alt=" photo 34p0sj9jpg_zps87d186ba.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>***Review edited after long deliberation and my inability to get this story out of my head. Any book that knocks my world off its axis deserves a five-star rating versus my initial no-rating. Nothing has changed but my revelation that this author deserves my five stars......</b><br><br>Now for my review.....<br><br>Sweet Jesus, gimme some Prozac, wine, anything to calm my nerves! I struggled so much with this book. Why? Because I hated "their" story yet I still think it's an exceptionally written book. It stirred so many emotions.....anger, sadness, angst, disgust but zero happiness. A fantastic book, yet a book I struggled to finish. What a major conflict, huh?<br><br>This is a story 100% revolving around DEPRESSION, LOSS AND BETRAYAL. Literally, that's the main focus, an all-consuming need to be with another man, to escape, to feel free when you've got the love of your life sitting home waiting for you. Catherine has struggled with miscarriage after miscarriage (yup, I said it. Everyone else dances around that as if it's some spoiler when it's divulged in the first chapter. That, to me is NOT a spoiler). Cathy is married to Ben, a stunningly handsome, wealthy, attorney and LOYAL partner. He too struggles with their child-bearing issues but continues to be the rock in the relationship- loving her through loss after loss.....<br><br>My Ben-<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Male%20Eye%20Candy/?action=view&amp;current=7de55ade9195d24c8217c806a9b8107f_zpsec284565.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433268i/871791._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Catherine is a successful hotel executive. When she meets her boss's 24-year old son he lights a fire inside of her that has long since flickered out. She's been existing in a marriage that's suffocating her....she just needs to breathe. Arsen provides that release. Arsen is her <i>kryptonite</i>.<br><br>My Catherine-<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Women%20for%20reviews/?action=view&amp;current=7b502142be2f44f7a233d1ee0af21268_zps7b06ac37.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390700i/752578.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Arsen is a spoiled, rich kid. He's used to having actresses and models on his arm, always being in the limelight. He's got to work to prove to daddy he's not lazy and is worthy of his inheritance. When he spots Cathy, his new "boss," he's found his newest conquest. Although something about her stirs more than his "manhood" (couldn't resist). He wants to be her friend. He wants to make her smile again. Friendship, can he, for once, do friendship?<br><br>My Arsen-<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Male%20Eye%20Candy/?action=view&amp;current=36554ed506f0de428452b6713399d27e_zpsef127e84.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434396i/876202._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As I said, through literally 75% of this book I struggled to hold on...just to finish it. It is 100% glorified angst. I wish I could say I empathized with Cathy but I didn't. Towards the end, I warmed up to her (when she finally pulls her head out of her ass) but that first 75%, I was seriously contemplating....<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Problems/tumblr_mlu246wDfD1rus9jso1_500_zps34cf0df7.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434396ra/876203.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mlu246wDfD1rus9jso1_500_zps34cf0df7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> (thanks for the gif Sue)<br><br>My thoughts on Catherine....<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/tumblr_lf99ydDf5W1qdus2g_zps92093ced.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434396ra/876204.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lf99ydDf5W1qdus2g_zps92093ced.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I seriously had huge issues empathizing with her character. Maybe had Ben been (ha) a douche, I could see it. Not sure. But she's not getting tears from me.....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/therethere-1_zps70cc60b3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434396ra/876205.gif" alt=" photo therethere-1_zps70cc60b3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Do I seem cold-hearted? Maybe. But I'm also a neonatal nurse that works DAILY with women who've went thru these exact issues and SUCKED IT UP. Get therapy. Everyone needs it sometimes in life. Don't self destruct.<br><br>My thoughts on Arsen....<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/340x-8_zps898b37bb.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434396ra/876206.gif" alt=" photo 340x-8_zps898b37bb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I know, no throwing stones at me but I seriously did NOT warm to him. He reminded me of an arrogant spoiled PUNK. The description when she first met him with his pants hanging low so his Armani band of his underwear was sticking out....ewe. <br><br>My thoughts on Ben....<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/FASSYletmeholdu_zps888407df.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434396ra/876207.gif" alt=" photo FASSYletmeholdu_zps888407df.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Ben...my heart wept for him.<br><br>So, is this a love story? Yes. A friend summed up this story great with one sentence and word of wisdom......<b>"Love the one you're with." </b><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=f76bebd54b5ed14fc9f61c0c165e322b_zps7401927e.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434396i/876208._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So, if you can stomach the mother of all love triangles where the guy that's getting cheated on is a DOLL and doesn't deserve it, this book is for you. I commend the author for this read. It pushes the reader beyond the limits one is used to in love stories. It's beautifully written and tugs at your heart at times (and makes you want to get a knife out to stab your e-reader at others). I'm happy I finished it and experienced it. The ending saved it for me. <br> <br>The best quote in the book-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=6dae079c75aa68672067c72360a03eb0_zps87823b08.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434396i/876209._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1160799207" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1160799207" />
    <a title="Peek At My Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review"><img alt="Peek At My Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1414761368p2/18263404.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1160799207?book_show_action=true">Jan 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Peek At My Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Peek At My Book Review" href="/user/show/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review">Peek At My Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review?shelf=2013">2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1160799207" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2194524489659220970"><b>Rating : 4 ‘Falling in love with the wrong person is easy’ Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421740106i/13410275.jpg' width='254' height='320' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> WARNING: Long Review Ahead!!! </b><br/><br/><b>My Views :</b> I was not going to rate this book because it tore my heart and crushed the pieces<b>...</b>, then after thinking about the story the whole night I actually changed my mind about the rating and Cathy…However this review is mostly my rant concerning this book and not a proper review, so my apologies beforehand. The story was wow and the writing just amazed me which should be enough for me to give thi</span>
  <span id="freeText2194524489659220970" style="display:none"><b>Rating : 4 ‘Falling in love with the wrong person is easy’ Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421740106i/13410275.jpg" width="254" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> WARNING: Long Review Ahead!!! </b><br><br><b>My Views :</b> I was not going to rate this book because it tore my heart and crushed the pieces<b>...</b>, then after thinking about the story the whole night I actually changed my mind about the rating and Cathy…However this review is mostly my rant concerning this book and not a proper review, so my apologies beforehand. The story was wow and the writing just amazed me which should be enough for me to give this 5 stars but I didn’t like the book, maybe because of the heartbreak.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421740011ra/13410250.gif" width="400" height="370" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Style of writing :</b> <b> AMAZING </b>…I just couldn’t out tis one down. It’s awesome how she makes her readers smile when she’s narrating the happy parts with Cathy and Ben and then makes you cry for the sad parts. She’s very good at both… <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421740011ra/13410251.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Characters :</b> Let’s talk about Ben first, I was team Ben throughout the book. He was such a <b> sweetheart to Cathy </b>even when they started dating then later on as a husband. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408899979ra/10909694.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> He was always caring and even though after 6 years of marriage he doesn’t even looks at other women except his wife. Ben was too perfect; <b> Cathy didn’t deserve someone like him. </b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421740011ra/13410252.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“Cathy, meeting you was chance, falling in love with you was destiny, and loving you is my reason to exist. I could tell you all the different ways I love you, but words are cheap. Instead, if you accept to be mine, if you let me be yours, I’ll show you for the rest of our lives how much you mean to me. Babe, I want to grow old with you. I want you to be the mother of our children, and I want you to be the last person I see before I take my last breath on this earth. I love you. Will you marry me and let my love for you make me the best man that I can be?”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/679835.gif" width="400" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then we have Arsen, the Manhattan’s New Favorite Boy who is broken on the inside but unfortunately started having feelings for a pregnant Cathy. I couldn’t bring myself to love Arsen because I felt like a big injustice was happening to Ben because of him as <b> he was the one who started it all.</b> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421740011i/13410253.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now Cathy was someone whom I both loved at the beginning and even sympathize with her but then at 50% I wanted her <b> BLOODY HEART ON A PLATTER. </b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421740011ra/13410254.gif" width="45" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> I couldn’t really understand why her feelings was <b> swinging back and forth between Ben and Arsen. </b> I just felt like Cathy was behaving as a child, she got a new toy named Arsen and the old ones seems to fade and she just want to play with him. I felt like it was just an infatuation, Arsen was attracted to her and Cathy already had a husband to loved her with his life so <b> she neglected that Love and focused on the new boy. </b> She wasn’t sure of what she wanted and no matter what happens her relationship with Arsen for me was purely a sexual one…It started with sex and ended with it. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421740011ra/13410255.gif" width="60" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But when I laid on the bed at night thinking, I felt like she wasn’t really wrong in her feelings because yes, sometimes we cannot bear the presence of the person that we love most because at that moment we are associating a certain pain/agony with that person and we do want a diversion. Unfortunately Cathy found that in Arsen and her mind was conditioned… <b> she wanted that peace that came with Arsen and she made the bad choice. </b> And this quote explains her situation so well…<br><br><b>
  <i>“The thing about being selfish is that you don’t care if someone is at your feet begging you to stay with him, offering you the world, his heart and soul. It doesn’t matter. You’ll do whatever you want to do. What you need to do for yourself. Nothing matters but what you want. What you think you need” </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421740011ra/13410256.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Favorite Part :</b> I love the <b> first meeting </b> of Ben and Cathy…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421740106i/13410276.jpg" width="309" height="451" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did not work?</b> To be honest when I started this book I knew only the blurb, I didn’t bother reading other reviews because I didn’t wanted to ruin it for me. Cheating is not something that bothers me in books but I couldn’t accept what was happening in this one. For me the injustice was towards (Ben) which made me drop some stars. I swear that <b> I’m not going to see cheating at the same angle now </b>…Mia Asher has ruined me for any other book that contains Cheating. Because at each point of the book all I was saying to Cathy was…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421740011ra/13410257.gif" width="400" height="310" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Similar books? </b> None that I have read and if there’s another like this one out there, <b> tearing my heart from my ribs will be less painful than reading that book!!! </b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421740011ra/13410258.gif" width="45" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> The only book that I pour tears so much was Beautiful Disaster but it’s not at all like this one…well except the heartbreak.<br><br><b> Recommended :</b> I have no idea if I want to recommend this one!!! <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421740011i/13410259.png" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://peekatmybookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="description" height="60" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418569189i/12827092._SX540_.jpg" width="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><a href="https://twitter.com/theVrsha" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="description" height="60" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418815952i/12909809.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://peekatmybookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="description" height="60" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418816316i/12909941.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Peek-At-My-Book-Review/313910035485042?ref=hl" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="description" height="60" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418815952i/12909811.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/100168723295071071120/posts" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="description" height="60" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418815952i/12909812.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

<div id="review_654128844" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/654128844" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/654128844?book_show_action=true">Jun 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=arc-s">arc-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer654128844" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13537303212475122407"><br/><i> **ARC provided by an author in exchange for honest review**</i><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1370958597l/17999935.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><br/>
  <b>
    <i> ‘How can something so wrong feel this right? Like it was meant to be?’</i>
  </b>
<br/><br/>Do you know the temptation of forbidden fruit? The taste of it? It’s hypnotizing, thrilling, captivating, you start to feel like deer in the lights, the need is so deep it runs through your veins, limbs, heart, you can’t breathe, and then suddenly it is just you and vivid imagination, <i>what if. </i><br/><br/>Why I’m asking this? Because of two things. Firstly, well,</span>
  <span id="freeText13537303212475122407" style="display:none"><br><i> **ARC provided by an author in exchange for honest review**</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1370958597l/17999935.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>
  <b>
    <i> ‘How can something so wrong feel this right? Like it was meant to be?’</i>
  </b>
<br><br>Do you know the temptation of forbidden fruit? The taste of it? It’s hypnotizing, thrilling, captivating, you start to feel like deer in the lights, the need is so deep it runs through your veins, limbs, heart, you can’t breathe, and then suddenly it is just you and vivid imagination, <i>what if. </i><br><br>Why I’m asking this? Because of two things. Firstly, well, my forbidden fruit, is Arsen. After reading blurb I knew it’d be bad idea to read this book. I freakin’ knew it! I hate love triangles and cheating, for god’s sake. I can’t handle them, I usually DNF a book with cheating. So why did I think requesting ARC of Arsen, would be great idea? I can’t even answer this question, I just saw this beautiful cover, interesting, however, dangerous for me blurb and I needed it. I started thinking about this novel all the time, totally mesmerized and captivated, silently waiting for a great occasion to try my luck. And yeah the freaky, red one with horns on my left shoulder won. <br><br>Secondly, Arsen is a novel about tasting Forbidden Fruit, it’s exactly about every painful stage: temptation, sin, punishment and redemption. Every one of them is agonizingly beautiful and truly excruciating. I have never experienced journey so raw, so primal and stunning to the core. I felt completely helpless and fragile while reading chapter after chapter loving this book more with every page and hating main character after her every sentece and action. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427227i/854057._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The story follows Cathy, woman who’s life is falling apart bit by bit. After being married to Ben for six years and after three miscarriages she feels it’s not her place in the world anymore. The burning passion for Ben is in ashes and she knows she can’t talk with him about her fear of not being woman enough. When she meets younger, full of life Arsen, her life goes upside down. <br><br>Arsen is typical love triangle with cheating involved, but at the same time it’s so much more. It’s the most bittersweet paradox in the whole world. I loved this book with every fiber of my being, but I still despised Cathy, the main character as well as Arsen. <br><br>She’s selfish, reckless, self centered, immature and plain stupid. I wanted so badly to connect with her and see her side of the story but the only thing I was able to see was broken woman who couldn’t understand what love really is. How much I loathed her is undiscribeable, but in a crazy way I know it’s how she’s supposed to be, and the fact Mia Asher could create her this way made me adore her more. In books, like in real life only likeable characters don’t exsist, someone has to be a villain. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427227i/854058._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Arsen is typical bad boy/ man whore. I suppose in other circumastances I would fall for him. But I couldn’t see him in good light when my heart ached for Ben, who really should get Husband of the Year Award. Sexy, caring man with golden heart who was brutally stabbed in the back. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427227i/854059._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Arsen is extremaly steamy read. I remember that Mia Asher asked me if I wouldn’t have issue with reading about hot, primal sex, because of my age (I’m 19). I told her „hell no! I love reading smut, there’s not a thing that could be to much for me”. But apparently I was a little bit too young to greatly appriciate this book. And it’s not about sex. It’s because I’ve never been in that long relationship to understand Cathy and Ben. The best thing is that I can read Arsen when I’ll be 30 and see this book in totally different light, which I know I will. <br> <br>But like I wrote affair is not all plot. In my eyes it’s more a psychological portrait of a cheater, than ordinary novel. I loved how easily author created her story. In the most stunning way Mia Asher told me about every stage of cheating aka Forbidden Fruit. I laughed, cried, pulled my hair and gritted my teeth. Few times I wanted to throw my ereader. If you liked Thougtless and are ready for something more mature Arsen will kick your socks off. <br><br>It’s so hard to find a modern not classical book which could give you the amazing feeling of katharsis. When your emotions run equal with author’s or characters. When their’s pain is yours, when their happiness make you giddy also. Arsen made me hate, made me love and forgive. That’s everything I have ever wished for. <br><br><br><i>More reviews on <a href="http://smokinhotbookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Smokin' Hot Book Blog</a> and my <a href="https://www.facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog?ref=stream&amp;hc_location=stream" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Page</a></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13537303212475122407" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText13183617971500522924" style="display:none">5 “You Are Mine” Stars!<br>*Recommended by Berry Nice*<br><br>-Sometimes not being in control, not being able to think, just losing yourself in the moment, is the greatest feeling in the world.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=34quy5v" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1519660989i/25126581._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" width="365" height="275" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Cathy meets Ben Stanwood when she’s 18 at college. He’s her soulmate &amp; the love of her life. They have been together 11 yrs., and married for 6 when they hit a rough patch they can’t seem to recover from. Lately Cathy feels broken inside, and like she can’t breathe. There’s an emotional disconnect that continues to grow between her and her husband. She meets a gorgeous guy named Arsen who she’s comfortable talking to. He’s someone who doesn’t judge her, and he makes her feel things she hadn’t felt in a long time. She can’t quit thinking of him, and eventually they cross that line. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=29479fm" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1519661050i/25126587._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" width="365" height="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-People say that if you play with fire, you'll get burned. Well, when it comes to Arsen, I not only want to get burned, I want to be incinerated.<br><br>-He's everything I need in this moment.<br><br>-He's like the sun. Blinding. I can't tear my gaze away, even as I'm being blinded by him.<br><br>-"How can something so wrong feel this right?"<br><br>-He's the air I need to breathe.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=16mcjo" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>My thoughts on this book are all over the place. I wasn’t sure if I loved it or hated it while reading because I felt so many conflicting emotions such as anger, heartbreak, sadness, sympathy, disgust, and lol, anxiety, but omg does this story make you feel! Obviously from the blurb you can guess it’s a love triangle. One woman who is in love with two very different men. One is a part of her soul, and the other brings her peace. I adored Ben. This man is everything beautiful a husband should be, which is probably why I found it hard to like Cathy. For most of the book I found her to be a self absorbed woman who feels little to no remorse for her actions. She basically sets fire to her life, and is left to deal with her regrets, mistakes, and consequences. <br><br>I loved both of these men, &amp; one is just as mouthwateringly delicious as the other, but my heart was shattered for Ben. I can’t say enough how much I loved this man! Absolute perfection!!! As much as this book leaves you feeling destroyed, I couldn’t get enough of this story, these characters, and this authors fabulous writing!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2586s5l" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>-I love him so very much that it hurts.<br><br>-I belong to her as much as she belongs to me.<br><br>-This tiny package of perfection has the power to completely destroy me, to annihilate me if she ever chose to. The funny thing is that I don’t give a damn about it. If it means that I get to be with her, to hold her in my arms, to call her my own for however long I have.<br><br>-Meeting you was chance, falling in love with you was destiny, and loving you is my reason to exist.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2r7rn9l" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_688867106" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/688867106" />
    <a title="Anna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8755560-anna"><img alt="Anna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1447951623p2/8755560.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/688867106?book_show_action=true">Aug 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna" href="/user/show/8755560-anna">Anna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8755560-anna?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8755560-anna?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8755560-anna?shelf=arc-august-2013">arc-august-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer688867106" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15513587819731832220"><b><br/>What a ride! <br/>A rollercoaster of emotions<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425005ra/847630.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> ** ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review ** </i><br/><br/>Arsen, Arsen, Arsen...<br/>After the first few pages it got me hooked, line and sinker and all. <br/>That was when I knew I was in for the ride. Where do I get from here? Well, first of all this is one of these amazingly broken stories as I use to call them, that you just don't go from to the next one right away but it occupies your thoughts for a while. But what's gotten to me at first was the sense</b></span>
  <span id="freeText15513587819731832220" style="display:none"><b><br>What a ride! <br>A rollercoaster of emotions<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425005ra/847630.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> ** ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review ** </i><br><br>Arsen, Arsen, Arsen...<br>After the first few pages it got me hooked, line and sinker and all. <br>That was when I knew I was in for the ride. Where do I get from here? Well, first of all this is one of these amazingly broken stories as I use to call them, that you just don't go from to the next one right away but it occupies your thoughts for a while. But what's gotten to me at first was the sense of humor. As it is I'm a real sucker for good laughing session and the story provided a lot of it side by side with other more heart wrenching emotions. Yes, I laughed and cried a lot. <br>What's more I totally liked the idea for introspection. It peaks your interest, makes you crave more when it's just gotten intense and then hello, sorry, come back in a chapter or two. Nice work ;) In addition the POVs and the Epilogue made the whole story so much more insightful.<br></b><br><i><br>"I didn’t fall in love. <br>I walked smack into it and then fell flat on my ass." </i><b><br>And she did, quite literally. <br><br>That's how the story begins. A girl meets a boy, they fall in love, get married eventually but...and yes, there's a lot of buts. </b><br><br><i>"If only I had known that years later we would suffer three miscarriages within a year, and then nothing, I think I would have questioned my words. <br>But I was young and in love, and like his grandmother told him, I felt like I could conquer the world with his love. <br>I felt invincible. <br>If only I had known that it takes a lot more than love to make a marriage work, then maybe our story would be different. <br>If only."</i><b><br><br>That's what the story is about. A lot of what-ifs and misguided life choices. All dressed in a beautifully broken love story. Don't get me wrong. I really, really liked all of it.<br><br>When the story catches up to the present, we're acquainted with Cathy, a broken married woman who starts to question her marriage and its future due to the pregnancies that ended all in miscariages. Her husband Ben strives to comfort her with his whole being but sometimes good intentions have unexpected consequences.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432211i/868016.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>"Sex is not a problem. Love isn’t either. I love Ben as much as the first time we said those three beautiful words to each other, but as each baby was taken away from my body by fate, by life, a part of me died and was buried with them in the cold-hard ground. The first miscarriage ripped a painful hole inside of me, the second one widened it, and the third just about broke me. <br>Time has fed that hole with inevitable boredom, monotony, and resentment towards life, Ben, and myself for not being woman enough. Enter doubt, and what you thought was an already rocky ride becomes a turbulence- ridden journey with no relief in sight except for the end. <br>The very end. <br>Doubts. They seep into your bloodstream, they plague every unused crevice inside your brain with revolving questions and no real answers. Is love a strong enough glue to put me back together again? Is the love between Ben and I strong enough to keep us together and our marriage afloat?"</i><b><br><br>Add temptation to the equation and you're in trouble, big trouble.<br>Meet Arsen.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794945i/598788.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Here we go...</b><br><br><i>"This guy exudes confidence and sex. I bet that if I got near him, trying to catch a whiff of his scent, I would be able to breathe in what pure sex smells like. Even his leisurely walk is sexy as hell. My God. "</i><b><br><br>He's the cause for her to abandon the voice of reason but also redefine herself. Does getting lost in the feeling mean actually getting lost? Or maybe it's a way for healing, finding new sense to live? Call her immature if you like but what I see is more of a call for help.</b><br><br><i>"Selfish me wanted Arsen, so I labeled him a friend when we were anything but. His teasing, his smiles, his touch… <br>It was never the same with anyone else. And I liked it. <br>No, I loved it. <br>I loved the attention he paid to me and the way he made me feel. Alive. <br>Happy. He made me forget. Ignorance is bliss, right? Well, knowledge is misery. <br>And the truth hurts. <br>Because it can’t ever be, it will never be."<br><br>" People say that if you play with fire, you’ll get burned. Well, when it comes to Arsen, I not only want to get burned, I want to be incinerated. " <br><br>" It always starts as a fun way to pass the time, light banter, innocent flirting…until it is not."</i><b><br><br>It's your decision how you choose to heal...<br>But better choose wisely...<br></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432211i/868017.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i><br>"Every action has a consequence. It doesn’t matter if you try to run or hide. It eventually it catches up to you. Call it karma if you must, but said karma can totally kick you in the ass. "<br><br>" And now I have to face the music. I have to make a choice once again. <br>And it doesn’t matter what choice I make. Which path I choose to follow. Either way, I will break my own heart. I will lose a part of myself. <br>But I think I already have. <br>I love two men. <br> And this time, the monster that I am, the one I’ve become, will bring someone else down with me. It’s the darkness in me, I tell you…It follows me everywhere I go, spreading like spilled black ink on white paper. "<br><br>"Dirty. I feel dirty. <br>I’m a cheater. <br>I’m scum."</i><br><b><br>What you don't quite anticipate is that you get a life lesson.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432211i/868018.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>"As cliché as it sounds, all I can do is learn from my mistakes.” </i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432211i/868019._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><br>My only regrets are the way things ended but there's only so much you can wish for. <br><br>I didn't quite expect how the story will end but that's even more encouraging. In my case it's when the story not only lives up to your expectations but exceeds them. With a hint of longing, wishing for more, I'm left wondering... What if?<br><br>I would recommend it to readers who love angsty stories.<br>Unlike <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13517535.Thoughtless__Thoughtless___1_" title="Thoughtless (Thoughtless, #1) by S.C. Stephens" rel="nofollow noopener">Thoughtless</a> or <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17158596.Collide__Collide___1_" title="Collide (Collide, #1) by Gail McHugh" rel="nofollow noopener">Collide</a> which are seemingly similar, it's a one book series and may leave some questions unanswered but it totally suits the whole story. <br> <br><br><br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://wicked-book-addict.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380374943i/729351.png" width="154" height="43" alt="View my blog" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br><a href="http://facebook.com/wickedbookblog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380374943i/729352.png" width="301" height="63" alt="Wicked Book Blog on Facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15513587819731832220" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/638818411?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer638818411" class="readable"
