<span id="freeTextContainer6139994968863322249"><b> 4 1/2 Stars </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424999i/847617.jpg' width='420' height='460' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First thing first, <b>YES</b> this book contains cheating. Now that that’s out of the way, Mia Asher can write! Will all readers relate to the main character, Cathy? No, not all will. I however related to Cathy and was sucked into this <b>LOVE TRIANGLE</b>. <br/><br/>The story contains, Cathy’s pov, Ben’s pov, past chapters which bring readers back to the beginning of Cathy and Ben’s relationship and Arsen’s pov . I found that the first 50% of the story was on the<b> SLOW</b> side but the last half of the book mo</span>
  <span id="freeText6139994968863322249" style="display:none"><b> 4 1/2 Stars </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424999i/847617.jpg" width="420" height="460" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First thing first, <b>YES</b> this book contains cheating. Now that that’s out of the way, Mia Asher can write! Will all readers relate to the main character, Cathy? No, not all will. I however related to Cathy and was sucked into this <b>LOVE TRIANGLE</b>. <br><br>The story contains, Cathy’s pov, Ben’s pov, past chapters which bring readers back to the beginning of Cathy and Ben’s relationship and Arsen’s pov . I found that the first 50% of the story was on the<b> SLOW</b> side but the last half of the book more than made up for it. This unbalance left me indecisive on rating the story. The angst and drama which kicks into full gear in the second half of the book was a nonstop thrill ride…at least for me. <br><br>Cathy’s psyche is slowly crumbling, she is bored and <b>BROKEN</b>. She has endured three miscarriages and the scars and feelings of inadequacy plague her and cause huge riffs in her marriage to Ben. Hey it happens it’s realistic even if her husband is amazing, which he kinda was. <br><br>Ben is written as one of those <b>PERFECT</b> guys, says all the right things, loves her to pieces and is sexy and hot in the bedroom. This is where readers will struggle with Cathy’s choices and back and forth feelings for the love of her life. <br><br>Yes, Ben is perfect, yes she loves him but then she meets…Arsen.<br><br><b>
  <i>" People say that when you play with fire you get burned. Well when it comes to Arsen, I not only want to get burned, I want to be incinerated. He’s my chance to be unguarded and content. To be wildly, incredibly, fiercely happy. " </i>
</b><br><br>Arsen is crude and unpredictable socialite playboy. He is twenty-four years old, he can’t hold a job down and he is just the complete opposite of perfect and of Ben.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I've seen the way you look at me. You want me, Catherine. So stop fucking lying to yourself. Shit, even when your perfect husband was sitting right to you at the bar, you could not stop staring at me."</i>
</b><br><br>Cathy and Ben face yet another devastating blow to their now fragile marriage. Communication is at a minimum and that Arsen is hot for Cathy. He is an in-your-face type of guy. I can see the majority of readers struggling to like him. I had MANY MANY moments myself but that’s not limited to Arsen even Ben I struggled with his failure to address but yeah he broke my heart as well…<br><br><b>
  <i>"Own me, fill me, break me, repair me, complete me. Do whatever you want to me. Just stay with me. I need you. I need to be able to live. I need my life back. I need you back."</i>
</b><br><br>Things get crazy and Cathy’s actions have consequences. Cathy seems selfish, immature while Ben has his head in the sand and Arsen can’t stand sharing. Since this story isn’t written by Olivia Cunning…a choice must be made.<br><br>This story has a couple of surprises at the end which made it original and for me unforgettable.<br><br><b>
  <i>”Falling in love with someone is easy. It’s loving when the newness has worn off, when life gets tough, when things get in the way, when physical passion is gone, that true love remains. When love can conquer it all.”</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="6139994968863322249" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1736122703" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3377139378104770655"><blockquote><b>Not sure how to rate this book because I actually read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17999935.Arsen_A_Broken_Love_Story' title='Arsen A Broken Love Story by Mia Asher' rel='nofollow noopener'> Arsen</a> back to back with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22449572.53_Letters_for_My_Lover__53_Letters_for_My_Lover___1_' title='53 Letters for My Lover (53 Letters for My Lover, #1) by Leylah Attar' rel='nofollow noopener'>53 Letters for my Lover</a> and had I not read the latter, I most certainly would have given this book a higher rating.</b><br/><br/>Notwithstanding, it was superbly written, and I dare say you will either love or hate it but I guarantee you won't be indifferent.</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText3377139378104770655" style="display:none"><blockquote><b>Not sure how to rate this book because I actually read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17999935.Arsen_A_Broken_Love_Story" title="Arsen A Broken Love Story by Mia Asher" rel="nofollow noopener"> Arsen</a> back to back with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22449572.53_Letters_for_My_Lover__53_Letters_for_My_Lover___1_" title="53 Letters for My Lover (53 Letters for My Lover, #1) by Leylah Attar" rel="nofollow noopener">53 Letters for my Lover</a> and had I not read the latter, I most certainly would have given this book a higher rating.</b><br /><br />Notwithstanding, it was superbly written, and I dare say you will either love or hate it but I guarantee you won't be indifferent.</blockquote></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_688809305" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/688809305" />
    <a title="Sara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10747133-sara"><img alt="Sara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1468189168p2/10747133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/688809305?book_show_action=true">Aug 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara" href="/user/show/10747133-sara">Sara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer688809305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6491187627782260050">What a powerful story.I know many don't like this for the cheating that takes place, and many feel hatred for Cathy. I was definitely angry with her actions, but I also felt bad for her.Yep, I said it. There will be no pictures, no gifs in this review. It's just me. Spoiler free, so I hope you read this whole thing. <br/><br/>Cathy- Did she cheat? Yes. Did she do some despicable things? Absolutely. But this book was more than her cheating. If you take a good hard look, its a situation that many women face</span>
  <span id="freeText6491187627782260050" style="display:none">What a powerful story.I know many don't like this for the cheating that takes place, and many feel hatred for Cathy. I was definitely angry with her actions, but I also felt bad for her.Yep, I said it. There will be no pictures, no gifs in this review. It's just me. Spoiler free, so I hope you read this whole thing. <br /><br />Cathy- Did she cheat? Yes. Did she do some despicable things? Absolutely. But this book was more than her cheating. If you take a good hard look, its a situation that many women face. Cathy I think had self esteem issues at a younger age. Bring on multiple miscarriages and you've got a woman in some serious world of pain. Every loss took a piece of her. Then she was emotionally pulling away from Ben. Add on top of that, the thought that she felt she couldn't talk to him. And lets face it, he did kind of shut her down, telling her she was being negative. All she needed was a shoulder, some time vent, and a steady listener. Don't mistake my words that I am excusing her behavior because I'm not. Cathy was mentally at a low place, and she was left wide open. It's likely that if it wasn't Arsen, it would have been someone else. Arsen was her high after being so low. It woke her up on the inside. It sparked her heart back to life. It was new and exciting. But what she didn't realize, he came with his own set of issues and a huge price. She thought she lost love and spark with Ben after all those years. Lots of loss and issues. Arsen was an escape from her hurt. I didn't doubt she still loved Ben. She just got lost. <br /><br />Ben- cant say a bad thing about him. He adored Cathy. Don't think it was lost on me the two scenes that happen on a street in the rain. Glorious. Although Ben was not perfect, he did not deserve all the pain he was dragged through. Could he have listened more? I'm sure. But he was always loyal and there wasn't a minute I didn't think he was devoted. I felt he would go to hell and back with her, and he did. Was I shocked towards the end at his admission? Yes, but I also saw how that was highly likely to happen as his world was no longer what he thought. The core of his existence had been rocked and was no longer steady. <br /><br />Arsen- well I think he truly liked Cathy. I'm not sure that I would ever have classified it as being in love. She saw him as a person and not a good looking man of wealth who she'd like to use and abuse. She was unavailable. He was wrong for going after her and pulling the lets be friends crap. He knew he had other ideas. The physical part of their affair didn't do the most damage. It was the emotional affair. I could feel it before they ever had sex. I knew she was in the red zone. I could see the train wreck happening. But once she crossed over into self destruct mode, Arsen was right there waiting with the net to catch her. It was heart wrenching. I never felt bad for arsen, he knew the score. Arsen was the fantasy and Ben was real life. And sometimes real life sucks and we want a break from it. I guess you could say he was a sort of predator. He knew she was feeling low. He was going for the kill shot. <br /><br />The things Cathy did were not ok. But as low as she was mentally, the sneaking around was exhilarating. It's what kept her going each day. The thrill. The excitement of the next text/phone call. Arsen could never have taken the place of Ben. There were many times I felt sick to my stomach at what she was doing. And if you really listened to her, she hated it to. She hated how she treated Ben. I think she hated herself but she shoved that way down because those feelings were too real to deal with. The most disgusting, the masquerade party. I wanted to puke. I felt she had hit rock bottom. She was so caught up in the fantasy of everything. Arsen was always a fantasy. Just a freakin fantasy. <br />So I guess I need to wrap it up. I'm glad Cathy got the crap end and did some suffering. I'm glad she got some help. I think that she learned a huge lesson in the worst possible way. Sometimes that happens. But also people make mistakes and deserve forgiveness and second chances. Not everyone will get one or both of those things. But could you imagine being hated for something that you did, that you live everyday with the guilt? <br />I would recommend reading this book with an open mind. I'm not condoning anything that she did. But look deeper than just her actions or the act of her cheating. There's more there. I'm glad the ending was the way it was. But I gotta tell ya, that epi with his pov i was like oh lord!<br /><br />Why 5 stars? Cause I felt every word on every page. I felt Cathy's disgust and remorse. I also felt her selfishness. I felt Ben's pain, his loss. I've been finished for hours and I can still feel this book. Job well done.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6491187627782260050" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1367102277" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1367102277" />
    <a title="Heather" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3829373-heather"><img alt="Heather" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1478521759p2/3829373.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1367102277?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather" href="/user/show/3829373-heather">Heather</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3829373-heather?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3829373-heather?shelf=more-please-to-reread">more-please-to-reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3829373-heather?shelf=triangles">triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3829373-heather?shelf=cheaters">cheaters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3829373-heather?shelf=aldiko1">aldiko1</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1367102277" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12802139859588189652"><b>WARNING!! I AM GOING TO GET A LITTLE PERSONAL!!!</b><br/>p.s. I don't think there are spoilers but just in case...<br/><br/>This is a wonderful story. You will feel so many emotions and you should be able to understand... Cathy and Ben have a perfect marriage. Both have amazing careers, a beautiful home, they're healthy and in love and have great family and friends. Unfortunately, they cannot have a baby. Cathy gets pregnant but loses the baby each time. It becomes devastating to their marriage...<br/><br/><b><i>"I love him. <br/> I’v</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText12802139859588189652" style="display:none"><b>WARNING!! I AM GOING TO GET A LITTLE PERSONAL!!!</b><br>p.s. I don't think there are spoilers but just in case...<br><br>This is a wonderful story. You will feel so many emotions and you should be able to understand... Cathy and Ben have a perfect marriage. Both have amazing careers, a beautiful home, they're healthy and in love and have great family and friends. Unfortunately, they cannot have a baby. Cathy gets pregnant but loses the baby each time. It becomes devastating to their marriage...<br><br><b><i>"I love him. <br> I’ve fallen in love with another man. But can you love two men at the same time? <br>Because I think I do."</i><br><br>Cathy,</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1507343600i/24108264._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>For the first half of the book I didn't like Cathy. She would justify her <i>serious</i> flirting with Arsen as harmless because he was only a "good friend". Yeah right. I know what MY husband is and isn't okay with. She knew too.<br>My story, I have had two second trimester miscarriages. The first I had to push out a two inch baby. The second one died inside and the doctor had to remove it from my body. When we got pregnant in 2013 we knew it was going to be our last attempt no matter how it turned out. Not until I was physically holding Logan did we relax. For myself, and Cathy, getting through the first trimester didn't mean safety. It was so stressful and terrifying but he made it. <br> I'm telling you my devastating story because I understood how Cathy was terrified and baby thoughts consumed her. All that is very real. I even could understand why she may do things that completely differ from her normal behavior, maybe do the wrong thing. HOWEVER, I did not blame my husband nor was I annoyed with him for, well, any reason.<br><br><b><i>"Late Sunday morning. I watch as my husband’s large and powerful body falls to the ground in surrender. <br>Broken…by me. <br>“I fucked Arsen,” I tell him quietly."</i><br><br>Ben,</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1507343600i/24108265._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I loved Ben so freaking much!!! Cathy was annoyed at his positivity but he was doing everything a husband should do. She <i>should have</i> known him well enough after that many years to know he wasn't cold hearted. That he was feeling the losses too. I never thought she treated him fairly. HOWEVER, I cheated on two perfect guys when I was younger and even though its so horribly wrong you look for a reason to cheat when you want one. I broke those two people too and reading Ben's POV was so sad knowing what I've done. <br>I don't like reviews stating Ben had no backbone. He adored his wife and wanted to save his marriage and I loved him.<br><br><b><i>"You know, I didn’t think I could fall in love again but—”</i><br><br>Arsen,</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1507343600i/24108266._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ohhh, Arsen. So vulnerable and easy to fall in love with. I found his possessiveness over "his" woman HOT! For the longest time I didn't find him serious, figured once he "had" Cathy he'd grow bored and move on. Let me tell you, Arsen PISSED me off around 83% but by the end of the book it was Arsen's POV that had my chest tight and the tears flowing. 💔<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445966786ra/16726954.gif" width="400" alt="description " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mia Asher did the impossible here... When it comes to love triangles I almost always pick the Arsen character, the new guy but as lovable as he was it was always Ben for me. I related to so many different parts of this book and I know it will stay with me for a very long time. I highly recommend it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12802139859588189652" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer9704831483487442942"><b>***5 stars with Dimples***</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395986751ra/9072966.gif' width='350' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Josh Holloway has nothing to do with this book, I just like his dimples</b><br/><br/>Okay... so what did I think about this book- <br/>I loved/hated/steamed/stewed/wept/tingled with excitement and was shocked by this story.   <span id="freeText9704831483487442942" style="display:none"><b>***5 stars with Dimples***</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395986751ra/9072966.gif" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Josh Holloway has nothing to do with this book, I just like his dimples</b><br><br>Okay... so what did I think about this book- <br>I loved/hated/steamed/stewed/wept/tingled with excitement and was shocked by this story. Or can you, can she? Do they truly love her back?<br><br><b>"My past, my present, and my future—my forever"</b><br><br><b>"I can feel again. I can see her face. I can touch her body next to mine"</b><br><br><b>“Yes. No…I don’t know. But for the life of me I couldn't stop reading this train wreck of a read..The emotions running through your heart/head are mind numbing..All I can say is that you have to have an open mind when reading this..If you want to read about puppy dogs and all those happy things this book isn't for you..Move along!! Run whilst you can!! <br><br>Cathy: The first miscarriage ripped a painful hole inside of me, the second widened it, and the third just about broke me, but the fourth killed me..<br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2iu6c9f" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>With Ben butterflies don't just flutter inside me, they ricochet like flying bullets..What went so wrong?? I also right from the get go loved all that was Ben!! Her rock, her everything, or so I thought!!<br><br>BEN<br><b> Love can destroy you<br>Love can erase you..<br>Love can heal you..<br>Love can reinvent you..<br>And, if you are lucky enough,<br>Love can make you whole again..</b><br>(That's what Cathy has done to me)<br><br>Such a hard book to recommend to anyone because of the taboo/cheating matter in this book, that's where you need to put all those negative feelings aside and just feel what the author is making you feel!! As I said I loved/Hated this book so the author did her job!! This book made me feel, it opened my heart and ripped it to shreds..Loved it!! <br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1043335574" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1043335574" />
    <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover"><img alt="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489089790p2/34338862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1043335574?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover">TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1043335574" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6257968187479530943">I don't know how to rate this. I'm torn between I loved it and I hated it. <br/><br/>What I loved? This makes you THINK. Makes you try to justify what's going on, makes you want to put yourself in Cathy's and Ben's and Arsen's shoes. Try to understand why Cathy does what she does.<br/><br/>What I hated? Well, Cathy. Yes, I hated her. She annoyed me, and she made me want to strangle her at times. Her actions were childish, her mind and thoughts were immature and she had some serious depression/compulsion issues. I t</span>
  <span id="freeText6257968187479530943" style="display:none">I don't know how to rate this. I'm torn between I loved it and I hated it. <br /><br />What I loved? This makes you THINK. Makes you try to justify what's going on, makes you want to put yourself in Cathy's and Ben's and Arsen's shoes. Try to understand why Cathy does what she does.<br /><br />What I hated? Well, Cathy. Yes, I hated her. She annoyed me, and she made me want to strangle her at times. Her actions were childish, her mind and thoughts were immature and she had some serious depression/compulsion issues. I thought Arsen was a petulant spoiled child looking for a new shiny toy to play with, and found it when he met Cathy. I don't like how she blamed Ben for her issues, and I don't like how she never once took his feelings into consideration, until she <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[decided to finally tell him she's been having sex with a younger man and up and left him <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. THAT's when the thought "hmm maybe Ben doesn't deserve this" finally crossed her mind. In all honesty, I didn't see her appeal. And I don't think she deserved Ben or even Arsen for that matter.<br /><br />BUT, somewhere along the way, Cathy wore me down, and I did feel a little bad for her. Maybe because she finally decided to own up to her issues and seek some help. And I have to admit, when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ben came back and they decided to work things out <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, I found myself reallyyyyy happy for them. I don't know how Mia Asher made my mind turn, but she did. <br /><br />AND THAT'S why I can't decide if I loved it or hated it. In the end, this story made me FEEL, even though the feelings weren't at all times pleasant.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6257968187479530943" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/3gK/fbQ62qn7jaats29hAju7jycjvwXuUxvVP0anLQONC5hIPrWNXe8+WILpXLaX6dIWj4WC6vW2JOBVkpt5w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FXp6DrUm0+kk0pYjGMBMnddHDARHMepJ5efHgepnYgvkNl6SYwzutvSAWdulqIPDgA6qYuWpHfWKcztUQTeTWA==')})
  }
